 Book: mandate-will of the People (non-fiction - English) Publisher: Westland limitededition: Paperback, 137 pages: 195 rupees The famous journalist, columnist and writer Veer Sanghvi has written a book
 sheershak he, mandet- vil of da pipal
 Sanghvi has written many such things in it, which are new and shocking to the public
 masalan indira gandhi ke bete sanjay gandhi ko indra kumaar gujral ne dapatate hue kya kaha, ye khud gujral kii jubaani bataaya gaya he
 Apart from this, it has also been told that Sonia Gandhi had decided in 1999 that if the Congress comes to power, Manmohan will be the PM
 babari masjid vidhwans ke maamle main raashtrapati kaa ronaa ho yaa america main ilaaj ke dauraan ek mulaakaat ke baad newclear deal par amar singh or phir sapa kaa badla stand, sanghavi ne tamaam ahm raajnneetik ghatnakramon ke kai dilachasp or nae byore die hai
 As editor for decades in various establishments and close penetration in the corridors of power, Sanghvi also knew many things that had not gone public
 ye kitaab aisi kai baton ko saamne laati hai
 Here are five interesting political developments from the book
 
 1
 sanjay gandhi ko gujral kii do took, varishton se tameez se baat kijieimergency kaa daur
 Indra Kumar Gujral Minister of Information Broadcasting in Indira Government
 ek cabinet meeting ke baad indira gandhi ke suputr sanjay gandhi kaa gujral ko farmaan
 i want to see All India Radio's news bulletin before it airs
 gujral ne do took jawaab diya
 This is not possible
 main bhi prasaaran se pehle kabhi nahin dekhtaa
 Then Indira comes and avoids the thing, see it later
 phir kuch roj baad gujral ko pradhanmantri awaas main talab kiya jaataa he
 When he arrives, he finds that Indira has left for her office
 unke saamne sanjay gandhi khadey hai
 Sanjay warns Gujral, "look, this won't work
" gujral ne wo jawaab diya, jiske bare main indira cabinet kaa or koi mantri soch bhi nahin saktaa tha
 Gujral said, see here
 jab tak main hum aise hi chalegaa
 And you will learn how to talk to superiors
 gujral yaheen nahin ruke
 He said that i have no accountability towards you
 main aapaki mummy kii sarkaar main mantri hum
 Saying this, Gujral left and then he was asked to resign
 2
 The Golden Temple of Amritsar in the shadow of the terror of Bhindranwale, Punjab 80s
 ek din punjab police ke diaiji attawal mandir jate hai
 Visit, get offerings
 vaapasi ke dauraan sidhiyon tak hi pahunch pate hai ki ek goli unke sharir ko bedh jaati he
 This bullet was fired by a terrorist of Bhindranwale's team
 jo mandir ke bagal ke guest house main apane bunker main ghaat lagaae baitha tha
 The sensation runs throughout the city, the whole state, the whole country
 sikhon ke is sabase pavitra ghar main is tarah kii harakat
 But shame was yet to set the scale
 police bal main bhindrawaale or uske gurgon kaa aisa khauf ki attawal kii laash bhi nahin uthaai ja saki
 His body remained on the stairs there for 24 hours
 phir amritsar kaa districtr magistrate bhindrawaale ke paas pahunchaa, gidgidaaya or tab usne attawal kii laash uthaane kii anumati di
 After this, the situation got worse and then the army carried out Operation Blue Star
 isamen bade paimaane par sainik, afasar, nirdosh tirthayatri, aatankwaadi or haa, bhindrawaale bhi maaraa gaya
 3
 ro rahe the raashtrapati shankaradayal sharma6 disambar 1992, dopaher 12
 At 30 o'clock, the nation came to know that the insane kar sevaks had climbed a dome of Babri Masjid in Ayodhya to break it
 dilli sthit tamaam muslim netaa pradhanmantri daftar main phone karne lage
 With hopes of intervention
 magar har baar jawaab miltaa, pradhanmantri aaraam kar rahe hai
 2 in the afternoon
 30 baje kai netaa, samajasevi or dharmaguru raashtrapati shankaradayal sharma se milane pahunche
 Sharma was crying
 unhone aae hue logon ko ek khat dikhaaya
 Sharma wrote this letter to Prime Minister Narasimha Rao
 isamen kaha gaya tha ki ayodhya main sthiti visphotak he, rajya kii bijepi sarkaar kii sthiti saaf nahin he
 In such a situation, the state government should dismiss and take the security system in its hands
 phir sharma bole, magar main bhi pradhanmantri tak nahin pahunch paaya
 It is also necessary to remember here that Narasimha Rao got the Prime Minister's chair only after Shankar Dayal Sharma's refusal
 darasal tamilnadu ke shreeperambudur main rajeev gandhi kii littey ke aatmghaatee hamalavar daste ke haathon hatya ke baad party main har koi unki vidhwaa sonia gandhi se netritv kii ummid kar rahaa tha
 Everyone asked him to become Congress president
 us vakt yah saaf tha ki jo party sanbhaalega, vahi satta main aane par pradhanmantri banegaa
 Sonia flatly denied this
 magar nayaa adhyaksh unheen kii sahmati se banataa, yah saaf tha
 Sonia consulted PN Haksar, an old family partner and bureaucrat
 hakasar ne uparashtrapati shankaradayal sharma kaa naam sujhaayaa
 Sharma refused, citing his ill health
 tab baari ai narsimha raav kii
 By that time, Rao had made up his mind to retire from politics
 rajeev gandhi kii good book main vah the nahin
 The situation was such that his Rajya Sabha MP was also over
 jab vah hyderabad jane ko taiyaar the, tabhi sonia ne elaan kiya
 Alright, it's PV Den
 or narsimha raav ko pehle party or phir chunaav nattejey aane ke baad desh kii kaman mil gai
 4
 mayawati ne chhue atal ke pair or phir diya dhokhprail 1999, atal bihari vaajapeyi kii sarkaar ko satta main 13 maheene biit chuke the
 Then the AIADMK of Jayalalithaa, an important ally of the alliance, withdrew support
 sarkaar alpamat main aa gai
 BSP supremo Mayawati, who was the chief minister in Uttar Pradesh with the support of the BJP, assured Atal's political managers that she would support the NDA
 us vakt ek-ek vot kii keemat thi
 On the day of voting on the trust vote, Mayawati went to meet Atal, touched his feet and spoke of the support of six party mps
 magar phir loksabhaa main mayawati palat gayi
 BSP mps voted against the NDA government
 sarkaar ek vot se gir gai
 Expressing happiness, Mayawati told the press, "I deliberately fooled the BJP
" 5
 It was only in 1999 that Sonia decided that Manmohan would be the PM of Congress
 In 1999, when the Atal government lost the vote of confidence by one vote, the ball came to the opposition's court
 sonia gandhi ne sarkaar banane kii koshishen tej kar deen
 Finally, Samajwadi Party chief Mulayam Singh Yadav vetoed this and mid-term elections were held in the country
 magar dilachasp yah he ki ab tak zyaadaatar log yah maanate the ki us vakt sonia ko pradhanmantri banane kii hadabadi thi
 Sonia is said to have submitted to President KR Narayanan both the list of letters of support and the claim to form the government
 magar raashtrapati narayanan kii maane to sonia gandhi khud pradhanmantri nahin bananaa chaahati thim
 He told Narayanan that if the coalition collects the required data for a majority, then he should administer oath to Manmohan Singh
 yani sonia 2004 main nahin, balki usase paanch saal pehle hi manmohan ko gaddi par baitaane kaa faisla kar chuki thim
 Perhaps in 1999, Manmohan Singh was contesting the Lok Sabha elections for the first and last time under this strategy
 magar, south dilli seat par vah bijepi ke vijay kumaar malhotra se 30 hajaar voton se chunaav haar gaye
 This book, written in English and from Westland Publication, is actually a by-product of a TV show by Veer Sanghvi during the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 sanghavi ke mutabik sho kii research ke dauraan maine paaya ki nai peedi ko bhartiya raajnneeti ke kai ahm padaavon ke bare main zyada jaankaree nahin he
 Keeping this in mind, this book was written
 isamen 1971 se 2009 tak ke chunaavon kaa byora or vishleshan he
 In this, instead of traditional statistics, Sanghvi has talked about the important characters, events and trends of those elections
 jo log bhartiya raajnneeti ko kareeb se dekhte hai
 There is nothing new in the book for him
 agar aapane veepi singh, natwar singh, sanjay baru, arady pradhan, pisi eleggender or aise hi kai lutiuns dilli ke kirdaaron kii aatmakathaayen or kitaaben padhi hai, to aapako kai kisse jane pahachaane lagenge
 But as Sanghvi himself said, my intention is to give this generation a simple language in the form of Indian elections and a look at Indian politics in the same order, rather than starting a new debate in political science and making big revelations
 kitaab kii bhashaa saral he
 The method is interesting and shaped such that it can be read only in one or two readings

 Human Resource Development Minister Smriti Irani said on Friday that German was a foreign language, yet it was being taught in Kendriya Vidyalaya, which violates the trilingual formula
 unhone kaha ki sarkaar ne jaanboojhkar sahmati patr (emoyu) par hastakshar nahin kiya
 Irani said here, 'according to this mou, German is described as the third language in all schools, which is a violation of the Indian Constitution, because it is not the third language of the country
 'irani ne kaha, 'jab yah naveekaran ke liye aayaa to na to maine or na hi mantralay yaa kendriya vidhyalay sanghathan ne emoyu par hastakshar kiye
 He said that the mou came up for renewal in September, while the dispute is being held in November
 mantralay ne kaha ki samvidhan kii aathvin anusuchee ke mutabik 22 anusuchit bhashaaon main german shaamil nahin he
 He said, 'as far as the students are concerned, the Kendriya Vidyalaya Sangathan is counseling the students from class six to eight
 iske alaava, chaatr jo bhi bhartiya bhashaa lenaa chahega vah use uplabdh karaayaa jayega
 The minister had earlier announced that the Kendriya Vidyalaya Sangathan has decided to discontinue the teaching of German language and teach Sanskrit as a third language
 unhone kaha tha ki yah nirnay deshhit main liya gaya he
 He has asked the Central School Board not to renew the 2011 mou with the Goeth Institute of the Government of Germany, which has provided 700 German teachers to the Kendriya Vidyalaya
 irani ne kaha ki emoyu bharat kii shiksha niti tathaa rashtriya shiksha ke dhaanche kaa ulanghan karata he
 The issue was raised by German Chancellor Angela Merkel in her first meeting with Prime Minister Narendra Modi during the G20 summit in Australia

 The Jnanpith Award is the highest award given by the Indian Jnanpith Trust for Indian literature

 Any citizen of India who writes in any of the 22 languages mentioned in the Eighth Schedule can receive this award

 Since 2012, the amount given as Jnanpith Award has been increased from Rs 7 lakh to Rs 11 lakh

 In the Indian freedom struggle, Sukhdev Thapar is a name who is known not only for his patriotism, courage and sacrifice on his motherland, but also as a unique friend of martyr A
 Azam Bhagat Singh
 britania hukumat ko apni krantikari gatividhiyon se dahala dene vaale sukhdev kaa janm 15 may 1907 ko punjab ke ludhiana shahar main hua tha
 From his childhood, he saw the oppression of the British rule in India and this was why he became a revolutionary to break the chains of slavery
 jawahar laal nehru vishvavidhyalay ke professor evam krantikariyon par kai pustaken likh chuke chaman laal ke anusaar hindustan socialist republican association ke sadsy sukhdev ke man main deshbhakti kii bhaavana kuta-kuta kar bhari thi
 He instilled a sense of patriotism among the youth at the National College in Lahore and inspired them to dive into the freedom movement
 ek kushal netaa ke rup main vah college main padhane vaale chaatro ko bharat ke gauravshaalee ateet ke bare main bhi bataaya karte the
 He along with other revolutionary colleagues started the Naujawan Bharat Sabha in Lahore
 yah ek aisa sanghathan tha jo yuvakon ko swatantraaa andolan main shaamil hone ke liye prerit karata tha
 According to historian Malati Malik, Sukhdev not only worked to instill patriotism in the youth, but also actively participated in revolutionary activities
 unka naam 1928 kii us ghatana ke liye pramukhataa se janaa jaataa he jab krantikariyon ne lala lajpat raay kii maut kaa badla lene ke liye gori hukumat ke kaarinde police upaadheekshak jepi sanders ko maut ke ghat utaar diya tha
 This incident shook the British Empire and revolutionaries were cheered all over the country
